  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_c5b72044-983c-4642-bc11-71c506ebb066'
      });
    }

  <span id="freeText3595629100890477407" style="display:none">Ashton is getting tired of being good, of impressing her parents and playing ideal girlfriend to Sawyer Vincent. Sawyer is perfect, a regular Prince Charming, but when he leaves town for the summer, it’s his cousin Beau who catches Ashton’s eye. Beau is the sexiest guy she’s ever seen, and even though he’s dangerous, Ashton is drawn to him.<br /><br />Beau loves his cousin like a brother, so the last thing he wants to do is make a move on Sawyer’s girl. Ashton is off-limits, absolutely. That’s why he does his best to keep his distance, even though he’s been in love with her forever. When Ashton wants to rekindle their childhood friendship in Sawyer’s absence, Beau knows he should say no.<br /><br />Ashton and Beau don’t want to hurt Sawyer. But the more they try to stay away from each other, the more intense their urges become. It’s getting way too hard to resist....</span>

<div class='communityAnswerBody'>
<div class='answererUserIcon'>
<a class="leftAlignedImage userPhoto" href="/user/show/35794089-caitlyn-books-are-my-life-baker"><img alt="" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/users/1534860001i/35794089._UY100_CR16,0,100,100_.jpg" /></a>
</div>
<div class='communityAnswerTextContainer'>
<span class='communityAnswererName'>
<a href="/user/show/35794089-caitlyn-books-are-my-life-baker">Caitlyn &quot;Books Are My Life&quot; Baker</a>
</span>
<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">It's amazing, wonderful, brilliant. It's not heavy - it's flirty Alabama fun with a love triangle and it's way better than the second book (as long as<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">It's amazing, wonderful, brilliant. It's not heavy - it's flirty Alabama fun with a love triangle and it's way better than the second book (as long as you're okay with two people who are totally meant for each other finally getting to be together even if it's at the expense of the boyfriend and cousin - yes, there's cheating, but I'm okay with that; it depends on if you are or aren't). I could sympathize with the main characters really well and loved this book a thousand times better than the second. <a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>
</span>
</div>
</div>

<span id="freeTextContainer6832263284271691725"><b><br/>DNF at 35%<br/><br/><br/>This was me from 1% to 30%<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380418056ra/827496.gif' alt='Image Hosted by ImageShack.us' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/>30-34%<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380418056ra/827497.gif' alt='Image Hosted by ImageShack.us' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/>35%<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380418056ra/827498.gif' alt='Image Hosted by ImageShack.us' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/>(except I didn't throw my reader through the window, only on my bed... but you get my point)<br/><br/><br/>Well I don't know what to say about this book other than I'm VERY disappointed in how the story went.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380418056ra/827499.gif' alt='Image Hosted by ImageShack.us' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/>From reading the blurb, I kinda got the idea this would be a forbidden love kind of thing, they were in love but couldn't be together cause she was dating his cousin for three years now.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380418056ra/827500.gif' alt='Image Hosted by ImageShack.us' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/><br/>No forbidden love here cause the MCs don't actually give a sh*t :D<br/><br/><br/>Don't know</b></span>
  <span id="freeText6832263284271691725" style="display:none"><b><br>DNF at 35%<br><br><br>This was me from 1% to 30%<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380418056ra/827496.gif" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>30-34%<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380418056ra/827497.gif" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" I'm VERY disappointed in how the story went.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380418056ra/827499.gif" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" cousin for three years now.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380418056ra/827500.gif" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br>No forbidden love here cause the MCs don't actually give a sh*t :D<br><br><br>Don't know why the boyfriend angle is even there cause it makes absolutely no difference with the relationship between Beau and Ash, only making them absolutely sh*tty characters for doing it.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380418056ra/827501.gif" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>But OK, I have to admit, I loved the first 30%.<br>Just loved, it was swoony, Beau is absolutely amazing and I wanted to read everything from his POV &lt;3 <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380735614ra/3116809.gif" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br>But then came Ash...<br>Let me tell you something about her.<br><br><br>She is dating Sawyer for three years, and doesn't want to have sex with him.<br><br>Newsflash woman, when that happens - YOU BREAK UP WITH THE GUY!!!!!<br><br>and NOT plan to have sex with a guy you re-friended five days ago.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380418056ra/827502.gif" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Ash made plans to have sex with Beau while her boyfriend is out of town with his family (he's a good guy btw).<br>And she made clear to Beau that she doesn't care about Sawyer and cheating him or just anything, she wants to have sex with Beau - BAD!<br>Beau of course can't help himself because he simply must be inside her ASAP.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380418056ra/827503.gif" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>So yeah, if it was done differently, I think it wouldn't bother me much, but Ash acting like a b*tch, planning to have sex with a guy she hasn't even talked to except for the last five days...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380418056ra/827504.gif" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>And I know a lot of people can read books where they don't like the main characters, but for me, both Beau and Ash went from love to hate in that scene, and I simply couldn't read a single page about them, I just couldn't!!! Gah!!!!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380418056ra/827505.gif" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br>And for me, this looks like a book written for adults who like to read YA, I know I'd certainly never ever recommend this one to an actual teenager, with such sh*tty main characters, no way!<br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380418056ra/827506.gif" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br></b></span>

<div id="review_1434308360" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1434308360" />
    <a title="Pearl Angeli" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/31514572-pearl-angeli"><img alt="Pearl Angeli" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1588420465p2/31514572.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1434308360?book_show_action=true">Nov 05, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Pearl Angeli" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Pearl Angeli" href="/user/show/31514572-pearl-angeli">Pearl Angeli</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/15852490-the-vincent-boys">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=2015-reads">2015-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=love-triangles">love-triangles</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=sobfest">sobfest</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=fangirling">fangirling</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=highly-recommended-na">highly-recommended-na</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=cute-book-couple">cute-book-couple</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=owned-physical-copy">owned-physical-copy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=hot-male-characters">hot-male-characters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=new-adult-contemporary">new-adult-contemporary</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1434308360" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13177853710124425819">I've buddyread this book with my lovely sistah <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1412311070?book_show_action=false' rel='nofollow noopener'>Beatrice</a>. (Click her name to read her beautiful review of this book) :)<br/><br/><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12900174.The_Vincent_Boys__The_Vincent_Boys___1_' title='The Vincent Boys (The Vincent Boys, #1) by Abbi Glines' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Vincent Boys</a> is a sweet and adorable NA story. It's light, quick, and easy to read. One of the reasons why I opted to read this book is because my love for <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/4872191.Abbi_Glines' title='Abbi Glines' rel='nofollow noopener'>Abbi Glines</a> is immense. I fell in love with her <b>Rosemary Beach series</b>, and although this book wasn't exactly as good as Rosemary Beach, it still surprised me.<br/><br/>I love <b>Ashton</b> and <b>Beau's</b> story. At first I was so skeptical beca</span>
  <span id="freeText13177853710124425819" style="display:none">I've buddyread this book with my lovely sistah <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1412311070?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">Beatrice</a>. (Click her name to read her beautiful review of this book) :)<br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12900174.The_Vincent_Boys__The_Vincent_Boys___1_" title="The Vincent Boys (The Vincent Boys, #1) by Abbi Glines" rel="nofollow noopener">The Vincent Boys</a> is a sweet and adorable NA story. It's light, quick, and easy to read. One of the reasons why I opted to read this book is because my love for <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/4872191.Abbi_Glines" title="Abbi Glines" rel="nofollow noopener">Abbi Glines</a> is immense. I fell in love with her <b>Rosemary Beach series</b>, and although this book wasn't exactly as good as Rosemary Beach, it still surprised me.<br><br>I love <b>Ashton</b> and <b>Beau's</b> story. At first I was so skeptical because of the love triangle thingy and the involvement of the major character <b>Sawyer</b> and especially the fact that there was cheating involved, but believe me when I say that all of these things did not matter as I've read the book because there was nothing seriously heavy about the story. The plot was simple and the peaceful setting was enough to make me feel warm and fuzzy inside.<br><br>This book was not perfect in terms of overall impact. The characters have flaws but the good thing is, there was an emotional depth in the story and there was a remakrable closure which made me smile in the end. And oh, who doesn't love a hot, gorgeous bad boy like <b>Beau</b> who does everything to protect his girl? *SWOONS! Overall, it's a nice guilty-pleasure and feel-good book-- something that basically cures reading slumps. I recommend this to NA lovers like me! :))<br><br>Rating:<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1445994440i/16731146.jpg" width="200" height="45" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><p>
  <a href="https://bibliopearl.wordpress.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1446199662i/16763926._SX540_.jpg" alt="Pearl's Book Journey (1)" width="380" height="190" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
</p><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1445993261i/16730770.jpg" width="200" height="120" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/230920941" />
    <a title="♥Rachel♥" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5481477-rachel"><img alt="♥Rachel♥" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1363996055p2/5481477.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/230920941?book_show_action=true">Nov 03, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="♥Rachel♥" class="user" itemprop="url" name="♥Rachel♥" href="/user/show/5481477-rachel">♥Rachel♥</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/15852490-the-vincent-boys">review of another edition</a>


          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to ♥Rachel♥ by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/3142322-bethany">Bethany</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5481477-rachel?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer230920941" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9528495465095682211">This is one <i>hot</i> and <i>steamy</i> story! Don't plan on doing anything else when you start this. I found I couldn't put it down! (I apologize up-front for the over usage of: !s and all-around gushing). <br/><br/>Ashton, Beau, and Sawyer were inseparable childhood friends. Beau and Sawyer, "the Vincent boys" are cousins, but its Ashton and Beau who are close. These two are the town's little hell-raisers, and Sawyer is the one usually bailing them out of trouble, and encouraging them to mend their ways. All this ch</span>
  <span id="freeText9528495465095682211" style="display:none">This is one <i>hot</i> and <i>steamy</i> story! Don't plan on doing anything else when you start this. I found I couldn't put it down! (I apologize up-front for the over usage of: !s and all-around gushing). <br /><br />Ashton, Beau, and Sawyer were inseparable childhood friends. Beau and Sawyer, "the Vincent boys" are cousins, but its Ashton and Beau who are close. These two are the town's little hell-raisers, and Sawyer is the one usually bailing them out of trouble, and encouraging them to mend their ways. All this changes though when both boys began to notice Ash in a different way. Sawyer is first to make a move, and Ash, thinking Beau isn't interested in her in that way, accepts him. So they've been the "perfect" couple for the last three years. He's the star quarterback, son of a respectable businessman (Beau's uncle), and always beside her at church on Sunday. Ash struggles to be the perfect girlfriend, always worried that she doesn't measure up to Sawyer. She squashes out the urges she has to have fun, go wild, and have some heat with her boyfriend. If she shows some of these urges, Sawyer does his best to squelch those tendencies. Beau on the other hand is as wild as he ever has been. He's the son of the "wild" Vincent brother, who died years ago. Sure he's on the football team, same as Sawyer, but he doesn't care what people think, and doesn't put up pretenses. Beau and Ash hardly say two words to each other anymore. However, when Sawyer goes on vacation with his family for the summer, Ash and Beau start hanging out all the time. Let the sexual tension begin, and OH, MY GOODNESS, prepare yourself for shirtless Beau!!<br /><br />I have to say that for a YA, this is <i>very</i> steamy! Beau is in the top five book-boyfriend category (yes, I know I'm pathetic)! I get weak in the knees just thinking about him. I just love everything that comes out of his mouth. I loved this scene: <br /><br /><i>
  <b>Beau's gaze made my cheeks flush. A pleased grin touched his lips and I suddenly wanted to know how those lips would feel pressed against mine. I couldn't take my eyes off them……"You're gonna have to stop doing that Ash," Beau whispered huskily and closed the space between us. His body was suddenly pressed against mine……."Ash, I'm trying real hard to be good…….Please remember I've got my limits and you studying my mouth like you want a taste is pushing me dangerously close to the edge of those limits."</b>
</i><br /><br />You wonder how this is all going to play out, because Ash is the girlfriend of Beau's cousin and best friend. Things were bound to get messy, and I worried that it would ruin the story for me. But I thought Abbi Glines did an excellent job handling this sticky situation. I have to say this is an excellent lesson for anyone dating. A guy/girl must love you for who you are, not who they want you to be. <br /><br />I highly recommend this for anyone who wants a fun, passionate read. I look forward to reading more from this author. <br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="9528495465095682211" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText1429527003281011829" style="display:none"><b>**** 4,5 stars ****</b><br /><br />Well, I didn't expect this... I thought it would be some sweet YA story, but it was quite hot, damn!, in those few sex scenes, Beau was deliciously dirty. <br /><br />Anyway, we have Ashton, who apparaently chose to date wrong Vincent boy few years prior. Now, her boyfriend (the good and proper one) Sawyer Vincent is out of town for the summer and she spends it with Beau Vincent - his cousin, the town bad boy. The three of them used to be best friends but ever since Ash and Sawyer started dating, Beau became distant. But it was Beau who was her partner in crime while doing crazy things when they were kids. While the summer goes by, Ash and Beau get close again, they rekindle their friendship and even more. Sawyer comes back and then there is drama… <br /><br />I was cheering for the bad boy Beau all the time because you can’t help but feel they are destined to be together.<br /><br />If you are into high school angst and Abbi Gline’s drama, this one will definitely work.</span>

<div id="review_228894361" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/228894361" />
    <a title="Shelly Crane" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5614044-shelly-crane"><img alt="Shelly Crane" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1359264053p2/5614044.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/228894361?book_show_action=true">Oct 29, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Shelly Crane" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Shelly Crane" href="/user/show/5614044-shelly-crane">Shelly Crane</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer228894361" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12824832467068303656">First off, Abbi Glines is amazing.<br/><br/>Secondly, ok, let's be real. <br/><br/>About half way through this book, I contemplated putting it down. Not that the story wasn't good, but because I was so emotional about it and I didn't see a way for anyone, not anyone, to have a happy ending. I was saying to myself, "Abbi, how dare you! You hook me and then break my heart!!" <br/>But of course, Abbi knows how to finagle a story. The way she brings all things in, all people, all walks of life makes for a beautiful story. T</span>
  <span id="freeText12824832467068303656" style="display:none">First off, Abbi Glines is amazing.<br /><br />Secondly, ok, let's be real. <br /><br />About half way through this book, I contemplated putting it down. Not that the story wasn't good, but because I was so emotional about it and I didn't see a way for anyone, not anyone, to have a happy ending. I was saying to myself, "Abbi, how dare you! You hook me and then break my heart!!" <br />But of course, Abbi knows how to finagle a story. The way she brings all things in, all people, all walks of life makes for a beautiful story. Though it may hurt me to read it all, it was beautiful nonetheless.<br /><br />Anybody who knows me at this point knows I don't like love triangles. I just don't like to read them, for some reason it doesn't sit well with me. I'm not terribly fond of Ash... Anyone who has the mentality of "I'm gonna do what I want to do because I've got to follow my heart and I don't care who's hurt in the process" grates me.<br /><br />BUT! :) <br /><br />She's real. She's human, she's just like thirty girls I knew in high school. She's just spent so long trying to please everyone but herself, trying to figure out how to make everything work in harmony, trying to be who everyone wants her to be, and for the love of all please her parents, that in the end she had no other choice but to rebel and blow up. It's one of those lessons learned.<br /><br />I'm so glad that I finished it and got to see how Abbi finished things up in a way that satisfied everyone as much as they could be. Sawyer was SOOO sweet in the end for someone who'd been betrayed that way. And Beau, gosh, you can't help but feel for him no matter the things he did before Ash. But I loved his protectiveness, even when she wasn't his. I love it when a guy is possessive in a sweet way. It was so real to me, it was like watching a movie. <br /><br />So thank you, Abbi. We all make mistakes, some extremely costly and stupid, some that hurt everyone involved and some that only hurt ourselves, but in the end the point is to learn from them and don't judge a book or person by its cover (no pun intended b\c the cover is gorgeous) and above all, you can't live your life with regret and hate. You just can't. <br /><br />5 solid, cry my eyes out, gripping my kindle with frustration, awesome stars from me.<br /><br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="12824832467068303656" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText8360710296836925129" style="display:none">I haven't written a review in... months, but I feel so strongly about this book I can't help putting down my opinion here.<br />Oh my.<br />Is this a book?<br />If it weren't from the fact that it was free I'd be pissed. And I thought it would be a safe bet.<br />Where should I start from? The tons of grammatical mistakes? And it's not like they were hinted at in a tasteful way, they were just NOT THERE.<br />A total disappointment.<br /><br /><br /><br /></span>

<div id="review_323018306" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/323018306" />
    <a title="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister"><img alt="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1486056026p2/4971692.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/323018306?book_show_action=true">May 02, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" href="/user/show/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister">Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781442486546" href="/book/show/16172220-the-vincent-boys">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister?shelf=love-triangle">love-triangle</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer323018306" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7651184933006877108"><b>4 Sexy Stars!</b><br/><br/><b>And THAT is how you handle a love triangle...</b><br/><br/>Abbi Glines astounds me! Her writing is so consistently <b>brilliant</b> and the excitement in turning that first page always makes me feel as if I'm unwrapping a gift. Her heroes display the perfect ratio of bad boy and sweetheart qualities...and those sexy Vincent boys are no exception! That said, I still find Abbi's characters to be distinct and vary considerably from book to book—never giving me the feeling that I've <i>met</i> a character before i</span>
  <span id="freeText7651184933006877108" style="display:none"><b>4 Sexy Stars!</b><br><br><b>And THAT is how you handle a love triangle...</b><br><br>Abbi Glines astounds me! Her writing is so consistently <b>brilliant</b> and the excitement in turning that first page always makes me feel as if I'm unwrapping a gift. Her heroes display the perfect ratio of bad boy and sweetheart qualities...and those sexy Vincent boys are no exception! That said, I still find Abbi's characters to be distinct and vary considerably from book to book—never giving me the feeling that I've <i>met</i> a character before in a different series. <br><br><i>The Vincent Boys: Extended and Uncut</i> basically takes the original story and spices it up with generous amounts of delicious, New Adult steam! If you're an Abbi Glines fan, you <i>know</i> just how detailed and realistic these jaw dropping, eye popping, mouth watering scenes are. Brilliant!<br><br><b>Ashton</b> is a preacher's daughter striving for perfection, but never quite feels connected to the innocent persona she's created in the hopes of pleasing her 'perfect' boyfriend, Sawyer. I loved seeing her growth in character, and her bumpy journey to self-discovery.<br><a href="http://s293.photobucket.com/user/kfuller5_2008/media/image_zpse3f3f366.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380376712i/731742._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo image_zpse3f3f366.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Sawyer Vincent</b> represents good and kindness; simplicity and safety. With the perfect parents and home life, he seemingly has it all--even the beautiful Ashton. <br><a href="http://s293.photobucket.com/user/kfuller5_2008/media/c6b95e3a-85fb-461d-b646-73c3fe81b57d_zps8f6b8687.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380376712i/731743.jpg" alt=" photo c6b95e3a-85fb-461d-b646-73c3fe81b57d_zps8f6b8687.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>Trouble can be a lot of fun. It's the straight and narrow that makes life tedious and boring.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><b>Beau Vincent</b> is known as the town bad boy with a solid playboy status and a heartbreaking upbringing. He stands for all which is opposite of his cousin Sawyer. These three have been friends since childhood until a betrayal threatens to tear them apart...<br><a href="http://s293.photobucket.com/user/kfuller5_2008/media/image_zps2c168c28.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380376712i/731744.jpg" alt=" photo image_zps2c168c28.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I'm usually not a fan of love triangles and all the drama and tension involved, but this one was executed perfectly. It's always easier when one character has a smaller role in the story, and when we are able to identify who is more obviously suited for the other; this tends to make the triangle more justifiable. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>I could live through anything if I could be promised that I'd always have this. Ashton in my arms. She was all I needed. Ever.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br>I loved the connection and passion between the characters and the way a simple kiss was transformed into a tantalizing, sexy love scene. This amazing story not only grabbed my attention, but allowed me to leave behind my own reality and just live in the world of the Vincent Boys for a while—and I love that about Abbi's writing. Looking forward to more of this exciting journey! <br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2mh7uop" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img height="50" width="50" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380347313i/701667.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><b>
  <u>Book Stats:</u>
</b><br><b>▪	 Genre/Category:</b> Romance/NA<br><b>▪	 Steam Caliber:</b> Extremely steamy.<br><b>▪ Romance:</b> Love triangle<br><b>▪	 Characters:</b> Well developed and layered.<br><b>▪	 Plot:</b> A well executed, tactful love triangle involving three teens who have been friends since childhood. <br><b>▪ Writing:</b> Steamy, descriptive, fluid. , <br><b>▪ POV:</b> 1st Person: Alternating perspectives <br><b>▪	 Cliffhanger:</b> None<br><b>▪	 Next Installment:</b> Follow up<br><br><a href="http://prettywordsbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412050368i/11316768.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="https://www.facebook.com/pages/Pretty-Words-Book-Blog/860331017317983" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img height='“40"' width="150" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1413062455i/11461733._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="7651184933006877108" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <a title="Beverly" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13095060-beverly"><img alt="Beverly" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1466964369p2/13095060.jpg" /></a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer520251642" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5828107448081787558"><b>* * * * * 5 <i>First Love</i> Stars * * * * *</b><br/><br/>Ashton, Sawyer, and Beau grew up together and were best friends. Beau always saw Ashton as his partner in crime, always up for some mischief, until the day everything changed…Sawyer asked Ashton out. <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392472826i/8566425.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>They were no longer the three amigos, and eventually Beau was pushed out. <br/><br/>Fast forward years later: Beau has turned into the town bad boy, Ashton is the perfect preacher’s daughter, and Sawyer is the perfect...everything. <br/><br/>Ashton, still dating Sawyer, is living l</span>
  <span id="freeText5828107448081787558" style="display:none"><b>* * * * * 5 <i>First Love</i> Stars * * * * *</b><br><br>Ashton, Sawyer, and Beau grew up together and were best friends. Beau always saw Ashton as his partner in crime, always up for some mischief, until the day everything changed…Sawyer asked Ashton out. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392472826i/8566425.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>They were no longer the three amigos, and eventually Beau was pushed out. <br><br>Fast forward years later: Beau has turned into the town bad boy, Ashton is the perfect preacher’s daughter, and Sawyer is the perfect...everything. <br><br>Ashton, still dating Sawyer, is living life exactly like she thinks <i>everyone</i> wants her to, until some events make her question her choices.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1406115979ra/10506659.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>Vincent Boys</i> explores the summer that changed all of their lives. <br><br>This story is fun, sexy, and heartwarming. This is a reread for me and one of my favorite Abbi books. I love Beau and Ashton together. Beau is sexy, confident, protective, and a little crass. Despite being a little rough around the edges he brings out the best in Ashton. <br><br>I love a story with forbidden love, and Abbi didn’t disappoint with this one. If you haven’t read this yet, I highly recommend it. <br><br><b>
  <i>Buddy read with my girl and fellow Abbi lover Dayna!</i>
</b></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer295821216" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16747153484810446938">The Vincent Boys is simply fantastic. The story of a girl whose heart is torn between two boys, her perfect boyfriend Sawyer who is loved and admired by all and his cousin Beau, the local bad boy who is sexy and irresistible.<br/><br/>There are several reasons why I think The Vincent Boys is incredible and here are just a few of them.<br/><br/>Even though it is a YA book it is a lot more mature and sexy than most, so if like me you are on the higher side of the young adult age bracket (or are older than that) and a</span>
  <span id="freeText16747153484810446938" style="display:none">The Vincent Boys is simply fantastic. The story of a girl whose heart is torn between two boys, her perfect boyfriend Sawyer who is loved and admired by all and his cousin Beau, the local bad boy who is sexy and irresistible.<br /><br />There are several reasons why I think The Vincent Boys is incredible and here are just a few of them.<br /><br />Even though it is a YA book it is a lot more mature and sexy than most, so if like me you are on the higher side of the young adult age bracket (or are older than that) and are a little fed up with romance that is on the level of what a 13 year old would experience then this is perfect. (The new version has a few extra steamy scenes and is a full NA novel)<br /><br />Abbi Glines is amazing at writing beautiful romances which still have a strong plot. Every single aspect of her writing is excellent and you won’t find anything lacking. The characters are well developed, they have their good and bad points and they seem like real people (some I wish were real). Every second of the story seems so real and you can almost see it happening around you.<br /><br />Ashton is a pretty great main character, she starts off just wanting to please everyone and be perfect but throughout the book you get to see her growth and development as she realises that is not the most important thing in life.<br /><br />Finally, the best thing about this book and why reading it isn’t an option but a necessity, Beau Vincent. The guy is just hot. Each snarky, sexy word out of his mouth will make you weak at the knees and you will wish you were Ashton. In fact you will wish that he was real. He is truly just the ultimate bad boy that all bad boys in any future book should be based on. <br /><br />I definitely recommend this book, it is one of my all-time favourites and I am sure that it will be yours too.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="16747153484810446938" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_556000638" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/556000638" />
    <a title="Rose" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3399699-rose"><img alt="Rose" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1386022874p2/3399699.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/556000638?book_show_action=true">Mar 08, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Rose" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Rose" href="/user/show/3399699-rose">Rose</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781442485259" href="/book/show/15851732-the-vincent-boys">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3399699-rose?shelf=realistic-fiction">realistic-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3399699-rose?shelf=mature">mature</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3399699-rose?shelf=multi-povs">multi-povs</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3399699-rose?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3399699-rose?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3399699-rose?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer556000638" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14274481625283254532"><b>Pre-read:</b> So apparently I'm going to end up reading this because I realized, in belated measure, that I actually *own* this book. (I honestly do not remember getting this at all - I guess it was either a Kindle Freebie or I got it for .99 when it was on sale, gah).<br/><br/>Would be against my nature to not read it since it's in my library, but here's to hoping it's better than I think it will be.<br/><br/><b>Post read:</b> I'm having a war of ratings between my head and my gut. My gut's telling me to rate this 1-star and</span>
  <span id="freeText14274481625283254532" style="display:none"><b>Pre-read:</b> So apparently I'm going to end up reading this because I realized, in belated measure, that I actually *own* this book. (I honestly do not remember getting this at all - I guess it was either a Kindle Freebie or I got it for .99 when it was on sale, gah).<br /><br />Would be against my nature to not read it since it's in my library, but here's to hoping it's better than I think it will be.<br /><br /><b>Post read:</b> I'm having a war of ratings between my head and my gut. My gut's telling me to rate this 1-star and unload about how much I detested the characters, the situations and the over-the-top melodrama. Not to mention the slut-shaming, the sexual harassment, the over-glorified sex-scenes, and the overarching misogyny and stupid, stupid actions of the characters. But my head's telling me that this really wasn't the worst NA title I've picked up and surprisingly, I read through this relatively quickly - I didn't put it down in the duration of reading it (unless I had to).<br /><br />I think my rating's in limbo (it'll be somewhere between 1 and 1.5 stars), but my thoughts on the book remain the same. It was pretty typical New Adult and I did not like the characters or the cheating measures. At least there were attempts at the characters trying to work out their issues. I just felt it was too much and unrealistic for what it had to offer. Plus so many things turned me off this that I've read handled better in more mature (read: in development) narratives. <br /><br />Yet another disconnect: there were times when I completely forgot this was a high school story - the characters seemed much older to me.<br /><br /><b>Full review:</b><br /><br />Turns out my head won the fight on this one, but barely. This is the first book I've read by Abbi Glines, and from the way that "The Vincent Boys" comes across, I'm not sure if I'm going to pick up another. I wasn't going to pick this one up originally from what some reviews had stated about the content (one of my friends even held strong comparisons of it to "Beautiful Disaster" by Jamie McGuire, which if many of you know, I had some very notable issues with that book and its respective sequel).<br /><br />I think what tipped the rating in this particular case was the fact that this book kept me reading, I didn't put it down the whole time I picked it up, and usually if it can keep my attention and hold it, it's doing something right *somewhere*. But there a lot of things wrong about "Vincent Boys" that bothered me to heck and back, so you might as well say - the 0.5 addition to this rating was only because it had a strong audio version (which I listened to in conjunction with my free Kindle copy - the only difference between the Extended and Uncut version with the original was that it had more sexy times, and that was to the detriment of the story, imho.)<br /><br />It takes place in a high school environment. Honestly, the characters seemed much older than that, particularly with the way the sexy times in this book were written. It shocked me that I kept forgetting that these characters were in high school. I guess it shouldn't considering the major mentions of their families having control in their lives and the bullying that Ash goes through later in the book, but there was a disconnect there in that this narrative felt like it was telling the stories of much older protagonists than teenagers, to me at least. <br /><br />Ashton is a preacher's daughter, the good girl with the seemingly perfect life, perfect boyfriend, perfect grades, perfect church attendance, perfect...well just about everything. (Yeah, I know. My Mary Sue radar was skipping off the tracks MANY times.) But Ash wants to be a "bad" girl, she doesn't think she's being honest with herself and just wants to let loose a bit.<br /><br />Normally I would be all for characters coming to terms with themselves and learning their respective life wasn't the one they wanted and they needed to find another route, but this book was all drama. I'll explain further.<br /><br />She used to be friends with the local bad boy (Beau), who's really close with Ash's current boyfriend (Sawyer, who just happens to be Beau's "cousin" if you will). When Sawyer's away, Ash and Beau kinda...well, "hook up" is a bit of an understatement. They rekindle their friendship and become lust heavy. They jump together faster than bunny rabbits, and their characters are so intensely unlikable that I just about threw my Ipod across the room - especially with the "I can, I can't have you, I'm jealous" go-betweens that constantly occur. When Sawyer returns, Ash and Beau do their best to keep their relationship quiet, but it's pretty obvious to everyone, except for Sawyer, that the two are growing closer.<br /><br />When the shoe finally drops, all heck breaks loose. And from there, it's a series of dramatic go betweens that have to do with Beau, Ash, and Sawyer getting caught in the whirlwind of revelations and cruelty games.<br /><br />I did see parts of this narrative that at least *attempted* to have the characters come to terms with the fact that there was a cheating relationship, that sentiments were realized and personal flaws exposed, but it felt like those were passing marks in comparison to the drama and its flares. Not to mention the many typical New Adult offenses - rampant slut shaming, sexual harassment (which at one point made the main character *cry*), bullying, misogyny, girl-on-girl hating, among other things. The religious stereotyping also really got to me in this book. It was like Glines took every possible stereotype you could have in the romantic scheme, plus added sex to the equation, and just pushed all of it into one lump of clay and tried to mold it only to come out with a sloppy result. It may have had its conflict resolution moments, but those were overshadowed by the obvious pandering towards the chosen relationship. That didn't sit well with me at all.<br /><br />I hated almost all of the characters, certainly the main three. Ash, Beau and Sawyer were incomprehensibly insufferable, but usually if I can follow a narrative where a character's train of thought and establishments are sound, I can get behind unlikable characters. I realize that you don't have to like the characters to like a story, I've picked up plenty of YA/NA books where I didn't necessarily like the characters, but I still followed them well because their establishments were sound. In Glines's narrative, I struggled with this. I thought there were moments where I could understand the pressures the characters were going through, but the story pulled the rug out from under me too many times with the overdrama and the obvious plot points trying to make the purported relationship work. It was manipulative. It didn't feel realistic.<br /><br />Overall, I couldn't recommend "The Vincent Boys" - the writing itself wasn't that strong (but admittedly it kept me reading to see what happened next), the story itself was over the top in its drama, and it just felt like it threw every cliche and every offense against the wall in New Adult that it could do, and then some. I didn't care for it. The only reason I give it an extra 0.5 star is because the audiobook narration was decent in performance from Kirby Heybourne and Shayna Thibodeaux, and because it kept me reading throughout. It's not the worst NA book I've read, but it had a lot of trigger points that rubbed me the wrong way.<br /><br />Overall score: 1.5/5</span>
  <a data-text-id="14274481625283254532" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_232258610" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/232258610" />
    <a title="Stacia (the 2010 club)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club"><img alt="Stacia (the 2010 club)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1417661051p2/4013351.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/232258610?book_show_action=true">Nov 06, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Stacia (the 2010 club)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Stacia (the 2010 club)" href="/user/show/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club">Stacia (the 2010 club)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=super-cheese">super-cheese</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer232258610" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1894997561053395985">2.5 stars. My low rating is only for some strange behavior quirks but <i>The Vincent Boys</i> wasn't a bad way to pass a couple of hours, even if the book had a few moments that I could have lived without. <br/><br/>For the most part, this was a quick, simple, and somewhat entertaining love story - with a few glaring flaws.<br/><br/><b>Beau</b> - He's the stereotypical bad boy in a stereotypical story. He's hot; he knows it; he flaunts it. Yet, he has a soft side because he carries a torch for the one girl he's always wanted but</span>
  <span id="freeText1894997561053395985" style="display:none">2.5 stars. My low rating is only for some strange behavior quirks but <i>The Vincent Boys</i> wasn't a bad way to pass a couple of hours, even if the book had a few moments that I could have lived without. <br /><br />For the most part, this was a quick, simple, and somewhat entertaining love story - with a few glaring flaws.<br /><br /><b>Beau</b> - He's the stereotypical bad boy in a stereotypical story. He's hot; he knows it; he flaunts it. Yet, he has a soft side because he carries a torch for the one girl he's always wanted but could not have. <br /><br />For a moment, I was having Cage and Willow deja vu, even though I knew this book came before <i>Because of Low</i>. I'm pretty sure when I eventually read Cage's book I'll have Beau deja vu.<br /><br />I am an admitted bad boy lover, but I don't think calling your promiscuous girlfriend a whore (multiple times) gives you an extra hole punch on the bad boy card. The previous sleeping around I get (as long as he's not attached, who am I to judge?) but insulting your <i>girlfriend</i> after you sleep with her? That's pretty low class. How about beating up on your cousin multiple times when not every situation needed to go that far? Hey, I like a protective man who will defend you by kicking ass as much as the next girl, but there's fine line between being protective and being a jackass.<br /><br /><b>"Girl you should've seen the bloody mess Beau made of Ryan's face. He beat the crap out of him. It was hot."</b><br /><br />Okay, so maybe Ryan deserved it. But when Beau turned around and did the same thing to Sawyer...eh. A small bitch slap would have sufficed. Rage beating someone when they didn't do anything except not stand up for another person is a bit extreme.<br /><br />That said, even with the shenanigans, Beau was still my favorite character because at least he had some sort of personality, flaws and all. It's hard not to be a little crazy about a romantic lead when you're reading inside of a guy's head and he's thinking about how much he wants this one person and would do anything to get her. This is why romance readers like romance, after all. The giddy feelings are fun.<br /><br /><b>Sawyer</b> - Yawn. He better go extra bad in book 2 because no one wants to read about a guy who has the personality of a postage stamp.<br /><br /><b>Ashton (Ash)</b> - Pretty blonde with curly hair, long legs, a tan, and a nice body - yet she thinks she's no beauty queen. Been there, read that. I think this character was recycled from <i>Breathe</i>.<br /><br />She strings along Beau for the sake of not wanting to hurt Sawyer. It's <i>Thoughtless</i> the junior version, complete with all of the crying and some of the blushing.<br /><br />This being the fourth book I've read by Glines now, I'm gathering that this author tends to write within her comfort zone. The characters and stories don't change all that much between series, other than little differences here and there.<br /><br />The editing errors were pretty noticeable. 'Your' and 'you're' were switched multiple times, as were 'to' and 'too.' It wasn't enough to take me out of story but I thought I'd include it in the review in case that is a factor for someone else.<br /><br /><b>So really...are there positives?</b><br /><br />Yes. If you like love stories that are easy to sink into and know that you'll get that happy little shiver over reading about a guy who will stop at nothing to keep the girl he loves safe, this book's probably a safe bet to work for you. The book is honestly not a bad read...it's just got some hiccups along the way. The story is nothing new or earth shattering, but entertaining doesn't always need to be. I enjoyed the read and still liked Beau for all of his misguided ways. I'll probably check out the next book just to see what trouble Sawyer can get into.</span>
  <a data-text-id="1894997561053395985" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_229247774" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/229247774" />
    <a title="Maida»-(¯`v´¯)-»" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3161105-maida---v--"><img alt="Maida»-(¯`v´¯)-»" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1555353893p2/3161105.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/229247774?book_show_action=true">Oct 30, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Maida»-(¯`v´¯)-»" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Maida»-(¯`v´¯)-»" href="/user/show/3161105-maida---v--">Maida»-(¯`v´¯)-»</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3161105-maida---v--?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3161105-maida---v--?shelf=paperback-or-hc-i-own">paperback-or-hc-i-own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3161105-maida---v--?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3161105-maida---v--?shelf=book-boyfriends">book-boyfriends</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer229247774" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9967450082181648640"><br/><b>RATING: 3.5-4 "Lucifer was Beautiful" Hearts!! :D</b><br/><br/><i>The Vincent Boys</i> is a cute and charming YA read, combining the best of drama, angst and romance as is customary with teenagers at the tender age of eighteen, and giving us a good story and likeable characters in its entirety. <br/><br/>Ashton is a heroine who is—to a certain extent—easy to understand and relate with despite her immoral and at times angering actions. She’s young and stuck between the love of two boys, and her dilemma to be with the one she l</span>
  <span id="freeText9967450082181648640" style="display:none"><br /><b>RATING: 3.5-4 "Lucifer was Beautiful" Hearts!! :D</b><br /><br /><i>The Vincent Boys</i> is a cute and charming YA read, combining the best of drama, angst and romance as is customary with teenagers at the tender age of eighteen, and giving us a good story and likeable characters in its entirety. <br /><br />Ashton is a heroine who is—to a certain extent—easy to understand and relate with despite her immoral and at times angering actions. She’s young and stuck between the love of two boys, and her dilemma to be with the one she loves and not hurt the other is believable. Although, <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[cheating is not something I like AT ALL. I wish that hadn’t been a part of the story <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. I love how she develops as a heroine, and makes her final choice based on what she wants and takes her time with that decision instead of just jumping in feet first with no care for anyone else’s feelings. Though, Beau helps her with that. Instead of being impatient and reckless, he takes a step back recognizing the position Ashton is in, and never once forces her to choose or makes her decisions for her. He is sweet, sexy and protective, and the two of them together are simultaneously hot, oozing sexual tension and just delightful. <br /><br />In spite of our helpless reaction to cringe every time there is a love triangle in a book, Ms. Glines doesn’t make us suffer, rather makes this trope work by making it easy for us to choose Beau over Sawyer as the victor of the battle of our hearts.<br /><br />Overall, <i>The Vincent Boys</i> is an entertaining and light read. I am definitely looking forward to Sawyer’s story next!<br /><br /><br /><br /><b>
  <i>Posted: September 4, 2015</i>
</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="9967450082181648640" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1412311070" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1412311070" />
    <a title="Beatrice Masaluñga" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4590441-beatrice-masalu-ga"><img alt="Beatrice Masaluñga" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1603719912p2/4590441.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1412311070?book_show_action=true">Oct 09, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Beatrice Masaluñga" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Beatrice Masaluñga" href="/user/show/4590441-beatrice-masalu-ga">Beatrice Masaluñga</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4590441-beatrice-masalu-ga?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1412311070" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11592165517024747612">Buddy read this with the lovely sis <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1434308360' rel='nofollow noopener'> Pearl</a> (Click the link to check out her fab review). <br/><br/>As always, Abbi Glines' novels are quick and easy to read. It never fails to get out of my reading slump. The story might be cliche but it's a guilty pleasure and I don't really mind love triangles. <br/><br/>Let's talk about the heroine: <b>Ashton Gray</b>. People recognized her as a preacher's daughter and as much as possible, she stays good in the eyes of many. She have been an obedient child to her parents and a perfect </span>
  <span id="freeText11592165517024747612" style="display:none">Buddy read this with the lovely sis <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1434308360" rel="nofollow noopener"> Pearl</a> (Click the link to check out her fab review). <br /><br />As always, Abbi Glines' novels are quick and easy to read. It never fails to get out of my reading slump. The story might be cliche but it's a guilty pleasure and I don't really mind love triangles. <br /><br />Let's talk about the heroine: <b>Ashton Gray</b>. People recognized her as a preacher's daughter and as much as possible, she stays good in the eyes of many. She have been an obedient child to her parents and a perfect girlfriend to Sawyer Vincent. Whenever she's around with <b>Beau Vincent</b>, the bad boy in their town who happens to be Sawyer's cousin, she feels carefree on who she really is. These three were best friends during their childhood years. They have an adorable friendship and it's really nice to see that bond. Things changed as they grew up when they boys see Ash differently. <br /><br />To be honest, I can't help but be annoyed with Ash. It's wrong to go behind Sawyer's back while he's away during Summer for Beau. Trying to understand her character, it's like she loved the wrong boy in the very beginning. I know it sounds wrong but at least she's honest about it. It's hard to be with someone but you're not really head over heels with that person. What she did is unforgivable, I like that she didn't set aside the issue. She had closure between the two guys and ended up with the <i>right</i>. I think it's enough for me to see that. <br /><br /><b>What really gets on my nerves: Ash's Father.</b> What kind of a preacher who calls someone a 'wild card' or a 'white trash'. How fucking judgmental. He maybe sorry about it but NAH. He reads a bible and should KNOW it's not good to judge someone. Sorry but it really ticked me off. <br /><br />Set aside the bad vibes. <b>I seriously love BEAU VINCENT</b>. Bad boys never failed to make me swoon and oh boy, I love Beau. The guy just fights for the girl he wants. He is a sexy, swoon-worthy bad boy. Overall, it's an enjoyable read and I really liked it.On the first half of this book, I'm decided to give it 3 stars but the last few chapters saved it. (Thank goodness!) #TeamBeauAlltheWay :) </span>
  <a data-text-id="11592165517024747612" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_232853296" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/232853296" />
    <a title="Laura" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4844873-laura"><img alt="Laura" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1299680097p2/4844873.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/232853296?book_show_action=true">Nov 08, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Laura" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Laura" href="/user/show/4844873-laura">Laura</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer232853296" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4184519022219487369"><b>4.5 Stars!</b> <br/><br/>Abbi Glines has a way with the boys! The Vincent Boys stole my heart and earned an all inclusive stay in my daydreams!<br/><br/>Beau, Sawyer, and Ashton shared trouble and love while growing up in a small, southern town filled with gossip, gossip, and more gossip. The Vincent family is the town’s star attraction and main source of gossip. Sawyer fills the all around Mr. Perfect, good boy role. Beau balances out the town with his beautiful bad boy reputation. Every town needs a bad boy—thank goo</span>
  <span id="freeText4184519022219487369" style="display:none"><b>4.5 Stars!</b> <br /><br />Abbi Glines has a way with the boys! The Vincent Boys stole my heart and earned an all inclusive stay in my daydreams!<br /><br />Beau, Sawyer, and Ashton shared trouble and love while growing up in a small, southern town filled with gossip, gossip, and more gossip. The Vincent family is the town’s star attraction and main source of gossip. Sawyer fills the all around Mr. Perfect, good boy role. Beau balances out the town with his beautiful bad boy reputation. Every town needs a bad boy—thank goodness! The boy makes senior citizens stop and stare! :D And then there was Ashton—the preacher’s daughter. Yes, I said preacher’s daughter! Giggle, giggle. I love this book! You stir those three up with love, gossip, and a fair amount of steamy attraction and tension—well you get one HOT story!<br /><br />This story was filled with romance and sexual tension, but a lot was going on underneath as well. Strong themes of being true to yourself and looking beyond one’s reputation are developed and explored with all the characters. Ashton’s character especially showed readers how easy it is to get lost in someone else’s shadow or image. Hold on to who you are and be yourself are two strong and wonderful messages for readers of any age to embrace.<br /><br />With just the right amount of southern hospitality and small town cattiness, this story creates a warm and cozy world that will pull you right in. Ms. Glines uses the open land, swimming holes, and southern heat all to her advantage. A shirtless Beau will make your belly flip flop! My stomach dropped a few times whenever Beau put his feelings about Ashton and Sawyer into words. He has this warm, but fierce way with words and emotions. I do feel like readers get a bit jipped concerning Beau’s view and feelings with a major development near the end of the book though. But we always want more—it’s a sign of a strong book and author. Always leave us wanting more!<br /><br />The Vincent Boys will make you swoon, smile, and never look at a stick shift quite the same way again! Have fun with the boys, y’all. I know I did. :D<br /><br />Favorite Quote:<br />“Mom has always told me Lucifer was beautiful.”<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="4184519022219487369" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_429914653" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/429914653" />
    <a title="Smitten&#39;s Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog"><img alt="Smitten&#39;s Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1429608146p2/12994342.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/429914653?book_show_action=true">Oct 08, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Smitten&#39;s Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Smitten&#39;s Book Blog" href="/user/show/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog">Smitten&#39;s Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=amazing-sexual-tension">amazing-sexual-tension</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog?shelf=bad-boy">bad-boy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer429914653" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13200187862373755024"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380393648i/757890._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380393648i/757891._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Aaah, I feel so bad for loving such a morally wrong book! Lol! I know I shouldn't want characters to be deceptive, cheating and hurtful, but I looove Ashton and Beau together!<br/><br/>My heart did break for Sawyer though. Just needed to put that out there, before I condemn myself as a cold hearted bitch. Oh, bless Sawyer. He did nothing wrong, he was a sweet, kind, gorgeous, loving boyfriend and they hurt him. :( I do feel, strongly, in real life, that there is no excuse for infidelity and lies, like tho</span>
  <span id="freeText13200187862373755024" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380393648i/757890._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380393648i/757891._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Aaah, I feel so bad for loving such a morally wrong book! Lol! I know I shouldn't want characters to be deceptive, cheating and hurtful, but I looove Ashton and Beau together!<br><br>My heart did break for Sawyer though. Just needed to put that out there, before I condemn myself as a cold hearted bitch. Oh, bless Sawyer. He did nothing wrong, he was a sweet, kind, gorgeous, loving boyfriend and they hurt him. :( I do feel, strongly, in real life, that there is no excuse for infidelity and lies, like those of Ash and Beau's, but my God does it make for a good read.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“Trouble can be a lot of fun. It's the straight and narrow that makes life tedious and boring.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>The sexual tension was palpable. <i>The Vincent Boys</i> made me heart race, it put knots in my stomach and a lump in my throat, on numerous occasions.<br><br>I really wondered if I might struggle to like Ashton, when I realised the direction the story was headed, but for some reason, I didn't. I wanted her and Beau to end up together, despite feeling for Sawyer, and I can only attribute this empathy to great writing.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>Beau's arms slipped around my waist. I knew I should step away but I couldn't make myself. This was home. Being in his arms like this was where I found peace.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>I downloaded the uncut version afterwards, out of curiosity, and flicked to the good bits. It did make the story much more intense and it made me connect, with Beau particularly, even more. I felt his pain and his loss more, at Sawyer's return, and I felt his need at the ending, having read more detailed descriptions of what he and Ash had shared. I think it made quite a difference and just illustrates the power of a connection between two people sexually and the heightened intensity and complication of emotions that are brought about when sex is introduced.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“I needed, I needed...you." <br>"Don't tell me you need me." <br>"But I can't help it. I do”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>At the moment, I am Team Beau, but that's because I think Beau is right for Ashton. I have no doubt that after reading the next book, I will be Team Sawyer. I think it's safe to say that <i>both</i> of the Vincent Boys are pretty damn gorgeous and I wouldn't mind me either one of them. ;)<br><br>To read more reviews go to my Book Blog: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://smittensbookblog.wordpress.com/">http://smittensbookblog.wordpress.com/</a><br>Follow me on Twitter: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://twitter.com/SmittenSC">https://twitter.com/SmittenSC</a><br>Find me on Pinterest: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://pinterest.com/smittensc/">http://pinterest.com/smittensc/</a><br>Join in the chat on Facebook: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.facebook.com/groups/427743250626754/?fref=ts">http://www.facebook.com/groups/427743...</a></span>

<div id="review_1738721925" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1738721925" />
    <a title="Grace (LovingDemBooks) Z." class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9529085-grace-lovingdembooks-z"><img alt="Grace (LovingDemBooks) Z." src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1465754864p2/9529085.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1738721925?book_show_action=true">Aug 25, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Grace (LovingDemBooks) Z." class="user" itemprop="url" name="Grace (LovingDemBooks) Z." href="/user/show/9529085-grace-lovingdembooks-z">Grace (LovingDemBooks) Z.</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

A) I wanted to see if this Abbi Glines series would be better than the other series I read (due to all the hype around Abbi Glines books).   <span id="freeText1188666808491506715" style="display:none">Buy this book on: | <b>
  <a href="http://amzn.to/2bm35E7" rel="nofollow noopener">Amazon</a>
